  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer14457201280687168400">In 1998, Ben Carson saved his pregnant wife, Anne, from the ultimate evil. Now, in the summer of 2015, the future looks great for Ben and Anne. Their son Taylor is married to his longtime love, Jenny, and they are expecting their first grandchild. Their daughter, Molly, now almost seventeen, is a beautiful, intelligent teenager.<br/><br/>Life has never been better for the Carson fam</span>
  <span id="freeText14457201280687168400" style="display:none">In 1998, Ben Carson saved his pregnant wife, Anne, from the ultimate evil. Now, in the summer of 2015, the future looks great for Ben and Anne. Their son Taylor is married to his longtime love, Jenny, and they are expecting their first grandchild. Their daughter, Molly, now almost seventeen, is a beautiful, intelligent teenager.<br /><br />Life has never been better for the Carson family. But that is about to change. The disturbing dreams are back and Ben is terrified. The ultimate evil force has not forgotten what Ben took from him and he is back in human form seeking revenge with the help of a handsome young man who befriends Molly and infiltrates the Carson family. This sequel to The Well House takes the reader on another incredible journey through the depths of the underworld to the gates of hell. Familiar characters return to help Ben on his journey together with a wizard, a shape shifter and a Basque priest.<br /><br />Ben, together with his wife Anne, his dog and his friends encounter terrifying creatures on their arduous journey to defeat evil and save the family. The Well House II: The Revenge is part drama and part fantasy and continues the exciting, unique and thoughtful story of a man's fight against the ultimate evil. Will Ben be victorious again or will he and his family be destroyed?</span>
  <a data-text-id="14457201280687168400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer3190828246086644401">This is the sequel to The Well House and Ben is again forced to save his family from the ultimate evil that he escaped from many years earlier.<br/><br/>After reading and thoroughly enjoying the first book in the series "The Well House" I couldn't wait to get started on this, the second book in the series. A clever plot with some of the same likeable characters, again this is a fast paced book that kept me keep on the edge of my seat! I really got immersed in this story and felt the horror and the shock w</span>
  <span id="freeText3190828246086644401" style="display:none">This is the sequel to The Well House and Ben is again forced to save his family from the ultimate evil that he escaped from many years earlier.<br /><br />After reading and thoroughly enjoying the first book in the series "The Well House" I couldn't wait to get started on this, the second book in the series. A clever plot with some of the same likeable characters, again this is a fast paced book that kept me keep on the edge of my seat! I really got immersed in this story and felt the horror and the shock which made me very jumpy!<br /><br />A very entertaining read that I think will appeal to a broader audience. Highly recommend.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3837355089519680704">After reading the first book in this series I was totally looking forward to reading The Well House II, disappointed? Absolutely not! it was even better than his first novel, fast paced, well written with amazingly captivating characters. The book had me on the edge of my seat with plenty of plot twists and turns. I highly recommend reading this book and cannot wait to get started on the next book in the series. 5 stars.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3104866258" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3104866258" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3104866258?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3104866258" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1312816095154325258">‘He was going to go crazy if Anne did not come back to him soon.’<br/><br/>Colorado author Michael S. Matassa earned his degrees from Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law and is an attorney and Municipal Court Judge in Arvada, Colorado. THE WELL HOUSE was his debut novel though he has also written several short stories and a screenplay. Now The Well House Series continues with THE REVENGE He states discovered the well house in the late summer of 1994, standing by a field of</span>
  <span id="freeText1312816095154325258" style="display:none">‘He was going to go crazy if Anne did not come back to him soon.’<br /><br />Colorado author Michael S. Matassa earned his degrees from Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law and is an attorney and Municipal Court Judge in Arvada, Colorado. THE WELL HOUSE was his debut novel though he has also written several short stories and a screenplay. Now The Well House Series continues with THE REVENGE He states discovered the well house in the late summer of 1994, standing by a field of corn on a small farm just south of Brighton Colorado, where it still stands today. His nom de plume is M.S. Matassa.<br /><br />The author’s skillful scene painting provides the curtain raiser for this novel – Deep in the lush forest in the Pyrenees Mountains, in a rustic cottage, a glass orb sat on its stand inside an oak cabinet in a locked room in the cellar. The pine needles swayed back and forth in the darkness as a gentle breeze blew through the trees outside, making a peaceful swishing sound. The orb was at rest, its milky liquid barely moving under the cool surface. About midnight a small dot of orange, no bigger than the tip of a pin, appeared deep in the center of the orb. As the dot grew, the milky liquid glowed with a pale orange cast, turning dark reddish-orange. The orb moved, ever so slightly, on its stand and then was still. Outside the cottage, the breeze grew stronger, and the peaceful sound became a howling gale.’ And it is this gift with prose that springs this story into life.<br /><br />The author’s synopsis reflects on the story that began in Volume I – ‘The ultimate evil comes to earth in a human body to carry out a sinister plan of retribution against the man who defeated him seventeen years earlier. In 1998, Ben Carson saved his pregnant wife, Anne, from the ultimate evil. Now, in the summer of 2015, the future looks great for Ben and Anne. Their son Taylor is married to his longtime love, Jenny, and they are expecting their first grandchild. Their daughter, Molly, now almost seventeen, is a beautiful, intelligent teenager. Life has never been better for the Carson family. But that is about to change. The disturbing dreams are back and Ben is terrified. The ultimate evil force has not forgotten what Ben took from him and he is back in human form seeking revenge with the help of a handsome young man who befriends Molly and infiltrates the Carson family. Familiar characters return to help Ben on his journey together with a wizard, a shape shifter and a Basque priest. Ben, together with his wife Anne, his dog and his friends encounter terrifying creatures on their arduous journey to defeat evil and save the family. Will Ben be victorious again or will he and his family be destroyed?<br /><br />There is a follow-up novel - THE WELL HOUSE III - and if it is of the caliber of the first two books then we have a powerful new author in our midst! Highly recommended – but keep the lights on. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1312816095154325258" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17136002872107057285">Reviewed by Sarah Stuart for Readers' Favorite <br/><br/>The Well House 11: The Revenge by M S Matassa is, as the title suggests, a sequel: it can be read as a standalone very easily due to the short synopsis at the start. It comprises a summing-up of Book 1, which ends, intriguingly, “but that was about to change”: a reference to the Ben Carson’s present peaceful life, and the entrance of a frightened living object, the Orb, signals trouble ahead. The battle between good and evil, where even Lucifer’s gr</span>
  <span id="freeText17136002872107057285" style="display:none">Reviewed by Sarah Stuart for Readers' Favorite <br /><br />The Well House 11: The Revenge by M S Matassa is, as the title suggests, a sequel: it can be read as a standalone very easily due to the short synopsis at the start. It comprises a summing-up of Book 1, which ends, intriguingly, “but that was about to change”: a reference to the Ben Carson’s present peaceful life, and the entrance of a frightened living object, the Orb, signals trouble ahead. The battle between good and evil, where even Lucifer’s grip on one of his key followers is loosened by the power of love, is intense, and fast-paced. The Carson’s extended family are endearingly normal whilst the opposition, not all with a common purpose other than the triumph of evil, is uncompromisingly malevolent. Can Ben win against the menacing force of retribution or must he pay the ultimate price?<br /><br />M S Matassa has created a fantasy flawlessly in The Well House 11: The Revenge; the reader is instantly immersed. Ben and Anne’s family life is so ordinary. Anne reassures Ben that his terrifying experiences are dreams, and takes him on vacation. An encounter with a raven, another “form” of evil, causes them to return home, where teenager Molly has fallen in love with Liam. The dog, Sherman, as well-drawn as the rest of the characters, senses that Liam isn’t “right”. Where does Thelma, mother of the keeper of the Orb, fit in? “Evil walked the earth, and it was close.” The threads of good and evil are intricately entwined in The Well House 11: The Revenge, weaving a tapestry that creates an incredibly dramatic fantasy. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17136002872107057285" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8011287999783445865" style="display:none">I loved the first novel in 'The Well House' series, so moved pretty quickly onto the second book, entitled 'The Revenge'. The plot takes place 17 years after the first novel, which followed Ben Carson's triumph against evil to save his wife and unborn daughter. In the 17 years that have passed, the Carson family has enjoyed a wonderful life, but evil is back for them. Ben will once again have to take another terrifying journey through the dark, encountering dangerous creatures and the forces of evil. What fate awaits for the Carson family at The Well House?<br /><br />MS Matassa has managed to write a sequel that is just as exciting and surprising as the original. Even though we have the same cast of characters and any of the same settings, the plot is still fresh and unpredictable. I read it in a couple of days and now I'm onto book three. Without giving too much away, I can't wait to find out what happens to Taylor in the third instalment of the series.<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText4646822112193872612" style="display:none">The Revenge, the second book by M.S Matassa is a great continuation from the first novel which I loved. I was excited when I found out that this book had been written. I am always worried if a sequel as good as the first book, but I was on the edge of my seat the whole way through this one and I struggled to put it down. This book kept me on the edge and it met all my expectations for a sequel. This is a great book for those who love adventure, as the Carson family provide plenty of that here. The author did a great job with the characters creating suspense and plenty of excitement. The characters is rich and established following the treads from book 1. I agree with what others have stated you will view your dreams differently. Looking forward to book 3…</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1308811117559963475">The Well House II: The Revenge by M.S. Matassa finds Ben Carson at peace with life. It has been over seventeen years since he fought the devil for his wife and daughter. But now the nightmares have returned. Satan has new tricks waiting for Ben and his family faces dangers in the most unusual places. Time will tell who gets the revenge; Satan or Ben Carson. The novel is a test of faith as old characters come together with new members to fight Satan.<br/><br/>M.S. Matassa resumes the fight between Satan an</span>
  <span id="freeText1308811117559963475" style="display:none">The Well House II: The Revenge by M.S. Matassa finds Ben Carson at peace with life. It has been over seventeen years since he fought the devil for his wife and daughter. But now the nightmares have returned. Satan has new tricks waiting for Ben and his family faces dangers in the most unusual places. Time will tell who gets the revenge; Satan or Ben Carson. The novel is a test of faith as old characters come together with new members to fight Satan.<br /><br />M.S. Matassa resumes the fight between Satan and Ben Carson in The Well House II: The Revenge. The story line continues along the original plot in this series, but finds Satan one step ahead of Ben. The pace is quick as Satan, aka Jack St. Louis, moves his plan into action rapidly and takes advantage of the element of surprise. Overall, the characters are rich, well-rounded, and keep the reader in suspense. Matassa keeps the reader on edge as the characters communicate through dreams and experience terrifying nightmares. You will view your dreams in a new light.</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9358082094443895221">This is the second book in the series called The Well House Chronicles written by M. S. Matassa. WOW! Seventeen years later Ben Carson's terrifying dreams are back. He feels and believes that the ultimate evil force was returning in human form and wants revenge for what Ben took from him. Again Ben must journey into the depths of the underworld into the gates of hell to save his family. But this time Ben has help from returning fascinating characters including several wizards! Aragon, Penelope a</span>
  <span id="freeText9358082094443895221" style="display:none">This is the second book in the series called The Well House Chronicles written by M. S. Matassa. WOW! Seventeen years later Ben Carson's terrifying dreams are back. He feels and believes that the ultimate evil force was returning in human form and wants revenge for what Ben took from him. Again Ben must journey into the depths of the underworld into the gates of hell to save his family. But this time Ben has help from returning fascinating characters including several wizards! Aragon, Penelope and Thelma are with him! His old friend, Claude, is called back as his dreams return him to Colorado to give everything he had to help Ben. Sherman, the loyal Golden Retriever, now much older still has the instincts that were crucial in protecting Ben so many years ago. The thrilling story is dark with twists and turns as the good again fights the evil. Could not put the book down! To me The Revenge was disturbing at times as I had grown to really like these vividly drawn characters and it was hard to realize that Ben had become more disparaging and melancholic. I'm glad I read the first novel. </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GMtMaRI3Ou1qQ1uhiwLcJkoLteUtlvtcJZd+io+PPXIi7SW7qWnzhc1o78B899b5nFRSLeMbdTt+6Tg7QszP6A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Q4KljA9L5t/manMtcjF+UcykPb0+UTjtg4VkVof1HVR5pMxetBUvt0FBx0yFxHSOGvvadfDctorY+yLnSrbvzg==')})
  }
//]]>

Her adjustment to a new culture includes shocking doses of American-style racial discr<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText11062613268497001941\" style=\"display:none\">In America’s Daughter, the second book of the trilogy, the author arrives in the United States in the company of Catherine Murray, an American high-school teacher. Her adjustment to a new culture includes shocking doses of American-style racial discrimination and Nhambu’s discovery that she must learn to be a Black American. She graduates from college, thus fulfilling her dream of becoming a teacher, and teaches high school in the inner city. She marries, has two children, and establishes herself in the American way of life. Then a visit to Africa, and especially to Tanzania, reawakens the drumbeats and dancing that she carries in her soul. On her return home, she teaches Swahili and African Studies, performs African dance at schools, and creates Aerobics With Soul®, a fitness workout based on African dance. She both finds and creates the family she longed for as a child and connects with her unknown background. The first book of the trilogy, Africa’s Child, was released in 2016. The final book of her memoir series—Drum Beats, Heart Beats—reveals more of Nhambu’s life as she searches for her father.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"11062613268497001941\" href=\"#\" They remain loyal to their men, because of complex, often unconscious forces.From mapping a path to power to laudable notions of holding the family together, Michaud examines the uniquely challenging <span id="freeTextContainer15084684227580248325">Michael S. Matassa is the author of The Well House, his first novel and several short stories. He was born in Dallas, Texas and now lives in Arvada, Colorado. Mr. Matassa is an attorney and a Municipal Court Judge. He attended Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law in Boulder, Colorado.<br/><br/>Mr. Matassa has finished a screenplay based on The Well House and is presently work</span>
  <span id="freeText15084684227580248325" style="display:none">Michael S. Matassa is the author of The Well House, his first novel and several short stories. He was born in Dallas, Texas and now lives in Arvada, Colorado. Mr. Matassa is an attorney and a Municipal Court Judge. He attended Regis College in Denver and the University of Colorado School of Law in Boulder, Colorado.<br /><br />Mr. Matassa has finished a screenplay based on The Well House and is presently working on a two sequels to The Well House. He writes under the pen name of <br />M. S. Matassa.</span>
